##### [Error- A Nil Value functoid is connected to a target node '{0}' which has child link(s).](core/error-nil-value-functoid-is-connected-to-a-target-node-which-has-child-link-s-.md)
##### [Error- The Scripting functoid, that connects to target node '{0}', has an error in its 'Xslt Call-Template' definition: '{1}'](core/error-scripting-functoid-has-an-error-in-its-xslt-call-template-definition.md)
##### [Warning- The Scripting functoid, that connects to target node '{0}', has a warning in its 'Xslt Call-Template' definition: '{1}'](core/warning-scripting-functoid-has-a-warning-in-its-xslt-call-template-definition.md)
##### [Error- The target node '{0}' has more than one unconditional Nil-Value functoid connected to it. Reduce the number to one.](core/error-the-target-node-has-more-than-one-unconditional-nil-value-functoid.md)
##### [Warning- The target node '{0}' has more than one Nil-Value functoid connected to it, with at least one being conditional. Depending on the input, the output may be incorrect.](core/warning-the-target-node-has-more-than-one-nil-value-functoid-connected.md)
